{/* MANUAL-CONTENT-START:intro */}
[Sportmonks](https://www.sportmonks.com/) is a sports data provider offering structured APIs for football, motorsport, odds, and reference data used to power scores, statistics, and betting-related applications.

With Sportmonks, you can access:

- **Football data**: fixtures, livescores, leagues, seasons, stages, rounds, teams, squads, players, coaches, referees, venues, standings, topscorers, transfers, schedules, commentaries, TV stations, rivals, expected goals (xG), and predictions
- **Motorsport data**: sessions, drivers, teams, championship standings, laps, and pitstops
- **Odds data**: pre-match and in-play odds, bookmakers, and markets
- **Core reference data**: continents, countries, regions, cities, types, and time zones

In Sim, the Sportmonks integration allows your agents to query fixtures, player and team statistics, transfer activity, standings, and odds directly within a workflow. Agents can pull expected goals (xG) by player or team, retrieve match commentaries and brackets, look up coaches and their histories, and enrich any of these with related data through the `include` parameterâ€”enabling workflows that build match reports, track transfer rumours, or surface live odds and predictions.
{/* MANUAL-CONTENT-END */}


## Usage Instructions

Integrate the Sportmonks sports data APIs into the workflow from a single block. Football: fixtures, livescores, leagues, seasons, stages, rounds, teams, squads, players, coaches, referees, venues, standings, topscorers, transfers, schedules, commentaries, TV stations, rivals, expected goals (xG), and predictions. Motorsport: sessions, drivers, teams, championship standings, laps, and pitstops. Odds: pre-match and in-play odds, bookmakers, and markets. Core: continents, countries, regions, cities, types, and time zones.



## Actions

### `sportmonks_football_expected_by_player`

Retrieve lineup-level expected goals (xG) values per player from Sportmonks

#### Input

| Parameter | Type | Required | Description |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Yes | Sportmonks API token |
| `include` | string | No | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response \(e.g. fixture;player;team;type\) |
| `filters` | string | No | Filters to apply |
| `per_page` | string | No | Number of results per page \(max 50, default 25\) |
| `page` | string | No | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | No | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

#### Output

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `expected` | array | Array of player-level expected goals \(xG\) entries |
|   â†ł `id` | number | Unique id of the expected value |
|   â†ł `fixture_id` | number | Fixture related to the value |
|   â†ł `player_id` | number | Player related to the value |
|   â†ł `team_id` | number | Team related to the value |
|   â†ł `lineup_id` | number | Lineup record the player relates to |
|   â†ł `type_id` | number | Type of the expected value |
|   â†ł `data` | object | The expected value payload |
|     â†ł `value` | number | The xG value |

### `sportmonks_football_expected_by_team`

Retrieve fixture-level expected goals (xG) values per team from Sportmonks

#### Input

| Parameter | Type | Required | Description |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Yes | Sportmonks API token |
| `include` | string | No | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response \(e.g. fixture;participant;type\) |
| `filters` | string | No | Filters to apply |
| `per_page` | string | No | Number of results per page \(max 50, default 25\) |
| `page` | string | No | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | No | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

#### Output

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `expected` | array | Array of team-level expected goals \(xG\) entries |
|   â†ł `id` | number | Unique id of the expected value |
|   â†ł `fixture_id` | number | Fixture related to the value |
|   â†ł `type_id` | number | Type of the expected value |
|   â†ł `participant_id` | number | Team related to the expected value |
|   â†ł `data` | object | The expected value payload |
|     â†ł `value` | number | The xG value |
|   â†ł `location` | string | Home or away |

### `sportmonks_football_get_all_commentaries`

Retrieve all textual commentaries available within your Sportmonks subscription

#### Input

| Parameter | Type | Required | Description |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Yes | Sportmonks API token |
| `include` | string | No | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response \(e.g. fixture;player\) |
| `filters` | string | No | Filters to apply |
| `per_page` | string | No | Number of results per page \(max 50, default 25\) |
| `page` | string | No | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | No | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

#### Output

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `commentaries` | array | Array of commentary entries |
|   â†ł `id` | number | Unique id of the commentary |
|   â†ł `fixture_id` | number | Fixture related to the commentary |
|   â†ł `comment` | string | The commentary text |
|   â†ł `minute` | number | Match minute of the comment |
|   â†ł `extra_minute` | number | Extra \(injury\) minute of the comment |
|   â†ł `is_goal` | boolean | Whether the comment is a goal |
|   â†ł `is_important` | boolean | Whether the comment is important |
|   â†ł `order` | number | Order of the comment |

### `sportmonks_football_get_all_fixtures`

Retrieve all football fixtures available within your Sportmonks subscription

#### Input

| Parameter | Type | Required | Description |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Yes | Sportmonks API token |
| `include` | string | No | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response \(e.g. participants;scores\) |
| `filters` | string | No | Filters to apply \(e.g. fixtureLeagues:501\) |
| `per_page` | string | No | Number of results per page \(max 50, default 25\) |
| `page` | string | No | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | No | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

#### Output

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `fixtures` | array | Array of fixture objects |
|   â†ł `id` | number | Unique id of the fixture |
|   â†ł `sport_id` | number | Sport the fixture is played at |
|   â†ł `league_id` | number | League the fixture is played in |
|   â†ł `season_id` | number | Season the fixture is played in |
|   â†ł `stage_id` | number | Stage the fixture is played in |
|   â†ł `group_id` | number | Group the fixture is played in |
|   â†ł `aggregate_id` | number | Aggregate the fixture belongs to |
|   â†ł `round_id` | number | Round the fixture is played in |
|   â†ł `state_id` | number | State \(status\) of the fixture |
|   â†ł `venue_id` | number | Venue the fixture is played at |
|   â†ł `name` | string | Name of the fixture \(participants\) |
|   â†ł `starting_at` | string | Datetime the fixture starts |
|   â†ł `result_info` | string | Final result summary |
|   â†ł `leg` | string | Leg of the fixture \(e.g. 1/1\) |
|   â†ł `details` | string | Details about the fixture |
|   â†ł `length` | number | Length of the fixture in minutes |
|   â†ł `placeholder` | boolean | Whether the fixture is a placeholder |
|   â†ł `has_odds` | boolean | Whether odds are available |
|   â†ł `has_premium_odds` | boolean | Whether premium odds are available |
|   â†ł `starting_at_timestamp` | number | UNIX timestamp of the start time |

### `sportmonks_football_get_all_players`

Retrieve all football players available within your Sportmonks subscription

#### Input

| Parameter | Type | Required | Description |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Yes | Sportmonks API token |
| `include` | string | No | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response \(e.g. nationality;position\) |
| `filters` | string | No | Filters to apply |
| `per_page` | string | No | Number of results per page \(max 50, default 25\) |
| `page` | string | No | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | No | Order players by id \(asc or desc\) |

#### Output

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `players` | array | Array of player objects |
|   â†ł `id` | number | Unique id of the player |
|   â†ł `sport_id` | number | Sport of the player |
|   â†ł `country_id` | number | Country of birth of the player |
|   â†ł `nationality_id` | number | Nationality of the player |
|   â†ł `city_id` | number | City of birth of the player |
|   â†ł `position_id` | number | Position of the player |
|   â†ł `detailed_position_id` | number | Detailed position of the player |
|   â†ł `type_id` | number | Type of the player |
|   â†ł `common_name` | string | Name the player is known for |
|   â†ł `firstname` | string | First name of the player |
|   â†ł `lastname` | string | Last name of the player |
|   â†ł `name` | string | Name of the player |
|   â†ł `display_name` | string | Display name of the player |
|   â†ł `image_path` | string | URL to the player headshot |
|   â†ł `height` | number | Height of the player in cm |
|   â†ł `weight` | number | Weight of the player in kg |
|   â†ł `date_of_birth` | string | Date of birth of the player |
|   â†ł `gender` | string | Gender of the player |

### `sportmonks_football_get_all_transfer_rumours`

Retrieve all transfer rumours available within your Sportmonks subscription

#### Input

| Parameter | Type | Required | Description |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Yes | Sportmonks API token |
| `include` | string | No | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response \(e.g. player;fromTeam;toTeam\) |
| `filters` | string | No | Filters to apply |
| `per_page` | string | No | Number of results per page \(max 50, default 25\) |
| `page` | string | No | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | No | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

#### Output

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `transferRumours` | array | Array of transfer rumour objects |
|   â†ł `id` | number | Unique id of the transfer rumour |
|   â†ł `sport_id` | number | Sport of the transfer rumour |
|   â†ł `player_id` | number | Player the rumour relates to |
|   â†ł `position_id` | number | Position id of the player |
|   â†ł `from_team_id` | number | Team the player would transfer from |
|   â†ł `to_team_id` | number | Team the player would transfer to |
|   â†ł `transfer_fee_id` | number | Transfer fee id of the rumour |
|   â†ł `probability` | string | Probability of the rumour \(e.g. LOW\) |
|   â†ł `source_name` | string | Name of the source of the rumour |
|   â†ł `source_url` | string | URL of the source of the rumour |
|   â†ł `amount` | number | Estimated transfer fee amount |
|   â†ł `currency` | string | Currency of the amount |
|   â†ł `date` | string | Date of the rumour |
|   â†ł `type_id` | number | Type of the transfer rumour |

| Parameter | Type | Required | Description |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |

| `per_page` | string | No | Number of results per page \(max 50, default 25\) |
| `page` | string | No | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | No | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

#### Output

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `transfers` | array | Array of transfer objects |
|   â†ł `id` | number | Unique id of the transfer |
|   â†ł `sport_id` | number | Sport of the transfer |
|   â†ł `player_id` | number | Player who transferred |
|   â†ł `type_id` | number | Type of the transfer |
|   â†ł `from_team_id` | number | Team the player transferred from |
|   â†ł `to_team_id` | number | Team the player transferred to |
|   â†ł `position_id` | number | Position id of the transfer |
|   â†ł `detailed_position_id` | number | Detailed position id of the transfer |
|   â†ł `date` | string | Date of the transfer |
|   â†ł `career_ended` | boolean | Whether the transfer ended the career |
|   â†ł `completed` | boolean | Whether the transfer is completed |
|   â†ł `amount` | number | Transfer fee amount |

### `sportmonks_football_get_brackets_by_season`

Retrieve the knockout-stage tournament bracket (stages and progression edges) for a season ID

#### Input

| Parameter | Type | Required | Description |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Yes | Sportmonks API token |
| `seasonId` | string | Yes | The unique id of the season |
| `include` | string | No | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response |

#### Output

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `brackets` | json | Bracket object containing stages \(fixtures grouped by knockout round\) and edges \(progression paths between fixtures\) |

### `sportmonks_football_get_coach`

| `filters` | string | No | Filters to apply |

#### Output

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `coach` | object | The requested coach object |
|   â†ł `id` | number | Unique id of the coach |
|   â†ł `player_id` | number | Player related to the coach |
|   â†ł `sport_id` | number | Sport of the coach |
|   â†ł `country_id` | number | Country of the coach |
|   â†ł `nationality_id` | number | Nationality of the coach |
|   â†ł `city_id` | number | Birth city of the coach |
|   â†ł `common_name` | string | Common name of the coach |
|   â†ł `firstname` | string | First name of the coach |
|   â†ł `lastname` | string | Last name of the coach |
|   â†ł `name` | string | Name of the coach |
|   â†ł `display_name` | string | Display name of the coach |
|   â†ł `image_path` | string | URL to the coach headshot |
|   â†ł `height` | number | Height of the coach in cm |
|   â†ł `weight` | number | Weight of the coach in kg |
|   â†ł `date_of_birth` | string | Date of birth of the coach |
|   â†ł `gender` | string | Gender of the coach |

|   â†ł `fixture_id` | number | Fixture the expected lineup relates to |
|   â†ł `player_id` | number | Player in the expected lineup |
|   â†ł `team_id` | number | Team of the expected lineup player |
|   â†ł `formation_field` | string | Formation field of the player |
|   â†ł `position_id` | number | Position id of the player |
|   â†ł `detailed_position_id` | number | Detailed position id of the player |
|   â†ł `type_id` | number | Type of the expected lineup record |

### `sportmonks_football_get_fixture`

#### Input

| Parameter | Type | Required | Description |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Yes | Sportmonks API token |
| `fixtureId` | string | Yes | The unique id of the fixture |
| `include` | string | No | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response \(e.g. participants;scores;events;lineups;statistics\) |
| `filters` | string | No | Filters to apply \(e.g. eventTypes:14\) |

#### Output

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `fixture` | object | The requested fixture object |
|   â†ł `id` | number | Unique id of the fixture |
|   â†ł `sport_id` | number | Sport the fixture is played at |
|   â†ł `league_id` | number | League the fixture is played in |
|   â†ł `season_id` | number | Season the fixture is played in |
|   â†ł `stage_id` | number | Stage the fixture is played in |
|   â†ł `group_id` | number | Group the fixture is played in |
|   â†ł `aggregate_id` | number | Aggregate the fixture belongs to |
|   â†ł `round_id` | number | Round the fixture is played in |
|   â†ł `state_id` | number | State \(status\) of the fixture |
|   â†ł `venue_id` | number | Venue the fixture is played at |
|   â†ł `name` | string | Name of the fixture \(participants\) |
|   â†ł `starting_at` | string | Datetime the fixture starts |
|   â†ł `result_info` | string | Final result summary |
|   â†ł `leg` | string | Leg of the fixture \(e.g. 1/1\) |
|   â†ł `details` | string | Details about the fixture |
|   â†ł `length` | number | Length of the fixture in minutes |
|   â†ł `placeholder` | boolean | Whether the fixture is a placeholder |
|   â†ł `has_odds` | boolean | Whether odds are available |
|   â†ł `has_premium_odds` | boolean | Whether premium odds are available |
|   â†ł `starting_at_timestamp` | number | UNIX timestamp of the start time |

### `sportmonks_football_get_fixtures_by_date`

#### Input

| --------- | ---- | ----------- |

|   â†ł `sport_id` | number | Sport the fixture is played at |
|   â†ł `league_id` | number | League the fixture is played in |
|   â†ł `season_id` | number | Season the fixture is played in |
|   â†ł `stage_id` | number | Stage the fixture is played in |
|   â†ł `group_id` | number | Group the fixture is played in |
|   â†ł `aggregate_id` | number | Aggregate the fixture belongs to |
|   â†ł `round_id` | number | Round the fixture is played in |
|   â†ł `state_id` | number | State \(status\) of the fixture |
|   â†ł `venue_id` | number | Venue the fixture is played at |
|   â†ł `name` | string | Name of the fixture \(participants\) |
|   â†ł `starting_at` | string | Datetime the fixture starts |
|   â†ł `result_info` | string | Final result summary |
|   â†ł `leg` | string | Leg of the fixture \(e.g. 1/1\) |
|   â†ł `details` | string | Details about the fixture |
|   â†ł `length` | number | Length of the fixture in minutes |
|   â†ł `placeholder` | boolean | Whether the fixture is a placeholder |
|   â†ł `has_odds` | boolean | Whether odds are available |
|   â†ł `has_premium_odds` | boolean | Whether premium odds are available |
|   â†ł `starting_at_timestamp` | number | UNIX timestamp of the start time |

### `sportmonks_football_get_fixtures_by_date_range`

| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `fixtures` | array | Array of fixture objects within the requested date range |
|   â†ł `id` | number | Unique id of the fixture |
|   â†ł `sport_id` | number | Sport the fixture is played at |
|   â†ł `league_id` | number | League the fixture is played in |
|   â†ł `season_id` | number | Season the fixture is played in |
|   â†ł `stage_id` | number | Stage the fixture is played in |
|   â†ł `group_id` | number | Group the fixture is played in |
|   â†ł `aggregate_id` | number | Aggregate the fixture belongs to |
|   â†ł `round_id` | number | Round the fixture is played in |
|   â†ł `state_id` | number | State \(status\) of the fixture |
|   â†ł `venue_id` | number | Venue the fixture is played at |
|   â†ł `name` | string | Name of the fixture \(participants\) |
|   â†ł `starting_at` | string | Datetime the fixture starts |
|   â†ł `result_info` | string | Final result summary |
|   â†ł `leg` | string | Leg of the fixture \(e.g. 1/1\) |
|   â†ł `details` | string | Details about the fixture |
|   â†ł `length` | number | Length of the fixture in minutes |
|   â†ł `placeholder` | boolean | Whether the fixture is a placeholder |
|   â†ł `has_odds` | boolean | Whether odds are available |

|   â†ł `id` | number | Unique id of the TOTW entry |

| --------- | ---- | ----------- |

|   â†ł `fixture_id` | number | Fixture related to the match fact |
|   â†ł `type_id` | number | Type of the match fact |
|   â†ł `participant` | string | Team the fact relates to \(home or away\) |
|   â†ł `basis` | string | Basis of the match fact \(e.g. h2h, overall\) |
|   â†ł `data` | json | Match fact data payload \(counts and percentages\) |
|   â†ł `natural_language` | string | Human-readable description of the match fact |
|   â†ł `category` | string | Category of the match fact |
|   â†ł `scope` | string | Scope of the match fact |

| `filters` | string | No | Filters to apply |

|   â†ł `stage_id` | number | Stage of the round |
|   â†ł `name` | string | Name of the round |
|   â†ł `finished` | boolean | Whether the round is finished |
|   â†ł `is_current` | boolean | Whether the round is the current round |
|   â†ł `starting_at` | string | Start date of the round |
|   â†ł `ending_at` | string | End date of the round |
|   â†ł `games_in_current_week` | boolean | Whether the round has fixtures this week |

### `sportmonks_football_get_schedules_by_season`

Retrieve the full schedule (stages, rounds and fixtures) for a season by season ID

#### Input

| Parameter | Type | Required | Description |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Yes | Sportmonks API token |
| `seasonId` | string | Yes | The unique id of the season |

#### Output

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `schedules` | json | Array of stages, each with nested rounds and their fixtures \(participants, scores\) |

### `sportmonks_football_get_topscorers_by_season`

#### Input

| Parameter | Type | Required | Description |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Yes | Sportmonks API token |
| `seasonId` | string | Yes | The unique id of the season |
| `include` | string | No | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response \(e.g. player;participant;type\) |
| `filters` | string | No | Filters to apply \(e.g. seasontopscorerTypes:208\) |
| `per_page` | string | No | Number of results per page \(max 50, default 25\) |
| `page` | string | No | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | No | Order topscorers by position \(asc or desc\) |

#### Output

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `topscorers` | array | Array of topscorer entries for the season |
|   â†ł `id` | number | Unique id of the topscorer record |
|   â†ł `season_id` | number | Season related to the topscorer \(absent on stage topscorers\) |
|   â†ł `league_id` | number | League related to the topscorer |
|   â†ł `stage_id` | number | Stage related to the topscorer |
|   â†ł `player_id` | number | Player related to the topscorer |
|   â†ł `participant_id` | number | Team related to the topscorer |
|   â†ł `type_id` | number | Type of the topscorer \(goals, assists, cards\) |
|   â†ł `position` | number | Position of the topscorer |
|   â†ł `total` | number | Number of goals, assists or cards |

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |

|   â†ł `player_id` | number | Player the rumour relates to |
|   â†ł `position_id` | number | Position id of the player |

|   â†ł `to_team_id` | number | Team the player would transfer to |

|   â†ł `source_url` | string | URL of the source of the rumour |
|   â†ł `amount` | number | Estimated transfer fee amount |
|   â†ł `currency` | string | Currency of the amount |
|   â†ł `date` | string | Date of the rumour |
|   â†ł `type_id` | number | Type of the transfer rumour |

| `filters` | string | No | Filters to apply \(e.g. fixtureLeagues:501\) |
| `per_page` | string | No | Number of results per page \(max 50, default 25\) |
| `page` | string | No | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | No | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `fixtures` | array | Array of upcoming fixture objects for the market |

|   â†ł `round_id` | number | Round the fixture is played in |
|   â†ł `state_id` | number | State \(status\) of the fixture |
|   â†ł `venue_id` | number | Venue the fixture is played at |

|   â†ł `starting_at` | string | Datetime the fixture starts |

### `sportmonks_football_search_venues`

### `sportmonks_motorsport_get_race_results_by_season_and_driver`

| `page` | string | No | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | No | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `results` | array | Array of stage objects for the season and driver, each including nested fixtures, lineups and lineup details |

|   â†ł `league_id` | number | League related to the stage |

|   â†ł `starting_at` | string | Starting date of the stage |
|   â†ł `ending_at` | string | Ending date of the stage |
|   â†ł `games_in_current_week` | boolean | Not used in the Motorsport API |
|   â†ł `tie_breaker_rule_id` | number | Not used in the Motorsport API |

### `sportmonks_odds_get_all_historical_odds`

Retrieve all available historical (premium) pre-match odd values from the Sportmonks Odds API

#### Input

| Parameter | Type | Required | Description |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Yes | Sportmonks API token |
| `include` | string | No | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response \(e.g. odd\) |
| `filters` | string | No | Filters to apply \(e.g. winningOdds\) |
| `per_page` | string | No | Number of results per page \(max 50, default 25\) |
| `page` | string | No | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | No | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

#### Output

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `historicalOdds` | array | Array of historical premium odd value records |
|   â†ł `id` | number | Unique id of the history record |
|   â†ł `odd_id` | number | Premium odd this history record belongs to |
|   â†ł `value` | string | Historical decimal odds value |
|   â†ł `probability` | string | Implied probability at this point in time |
|   â†ł `dp3` | string | Decimal odds to 3 decimal places |
|   â†ł `fractional` | string | Fractional odds |
|   â†ł `american` | string | American/moneyline odds |
|   â†ł `bookmaker_update` | string | Bookmaker's update timestamp for this record \(UTC\) |

### `sportmonks_odds_get_all_inplay_odds`

Retrieve all available live (in-play) odds from the Sportmonks Odds API

#### Input

| Parameter | Type | Required | Description |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Yes | Sportmonks API token |
| `include` | string | No | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response \(e.g. market;bookmaker\) |
| `filters` | string | No | Filters to apply \(e.g. markets:1,12, bookmakers:2,14, IdAfter:oddID\) |
| `per_page` | string | No | Number of results per page \(max 50, default 25\) |
| `page` | string | No | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | No | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

#### Output

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `odds` | array | Array of in-play odd objects |
|   â†ł `id` | number | Unique id of the odd |
|   â†ł `fixture_id` | number | Fixture the odd belongs to |
|   â†ł `external_id` | number | External id of the odd |
|   â†ł `market_id` | number | Market the odd belongs to |
|   â†ł `bookmaker_id` | number | Bookmaker offering the odd |
|   â†ł `label` | string | Outcome label \(e.g. 1, X, 2\) |
|   â†ł `value` | string | Decimal odds value |
|   â†ł `name` | string | Outcome name |
|   â†ł `sort_order` | number | Sort order of the odd |
|   â†ł `market_description` | string | Description of the market |
|   â†ł `probability` | string | Implied probability |
|   â†ł `dp3` | string | Decimal odds to 3 decimal places |
|   â†ł `fractional` | string | Fractional odds |
|   â†ł `american` | string | American/moneyline odds |
|   â†ł `winning` | boolean | Whether this is the winning outcome |
|   â†ł `suspended` | boolean | Whether the odd is suspended |
|   â†ł `stopped` | boolean | Whether the odd is stopped |
|   â†ł `total` | string | Total line for over/under markets |
|   â†ł `handicap` | string | Handicap line for handicap markets |
|   â†ł `participants` | string | Participant ids related to the outcome |

### `sportmonks_odds_get_all_pre_match_odds`

#### Input

| Parameter | Type | Required | Description |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `odds` | array | Array of pre-match odd objects |
|   â†ł `id` | number | Unique id of the odd |
|   â†ł `fixture_id` | number | Fixture the odd belongs to |
|   â†ł `market_id` | number | Market the odd belongs to |
|   â†ł `bookmaker_id` | number | Bookmaker offering the odd |
|   â†ł `label` | string | Outcome label \(e.g. 1, X, 2\) |
|   â†ł `value` | string | Decimal odds value |
|   â†ł `name` | string | Outcome name \(e.g. Home, Draw, Away\) |
|   â†ł `sort_order` | number | Sort order of the odd |
|   â†ł `market_description` | string | Description of the market |
|   â†ł `probability` | string | Implied probability \(e.g. 48.78%\) |
|   â†ł `dp3` | string | Decimal odds to 3 decimal places |
|   â†ł `fractional` | string | Fractional odds \(e.g. 31/15\) |
|   â†ł `american` | string | American/moneyline odds \(e.g. +104\) |
|   â†ł `winning` | boolean | Whether this is the winning outcome |
|   â†ł `stopped` | boolean | Whether the odd is stopped |
|   â†ł `total` | string | Total line for over/under markets |
|   â†ł `handicap` | string | Handicap line for handicap markets |
|   â†ł `participants` | string | Participant ids related to the outcome |
|   â†ł `original_label` | string | Original handicap value of the odd \(handicap markets\) |

| `apiKey` | string | Yes | Sportmonks API token |
| `fixtureId` | string | Yes | The unique id of the fixture |
| `per_page` | string | No | Number of results per page \(max 50, default 25\) |
| `page` | string | No | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | No | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

#### Output

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `bookmakers` | array | Array of bookmaker objects available for the fixture |
|   â†ł `id` | number | Unique id of the bookmaker |
|   â†ł `name` | string | Name of the bookmaker |
|   â†ł `logo` | string | Logo of the bookmaker |

### `sportmonks_odds_get_inplay_odds_by_fixture`

Retrieve live (in-play) odds for a fixture by fixture ID from the Sportmonks Odds API

#### Input

| Parameter | Type | Required | Description |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Yes | Sportmonks API token |
| `fixtureId` | string | Yes | The unique id of the fixture |
| `include` | string | No | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response \(e.g. market;bookmaker\) |
| `filters` | string | No | Filters to apply \(e.g. markets:1,12 or bookmakers:2,14 or winningOdds\) |
| `per_page` | string | No | Number of results per page \(max 50, default 25\) |
| `page` | string | No | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | No | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

#### Output

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `odds` | array | Array of in-play odd objects for the fixture |
|   â†ł `id` | number | Unique id of the odd |
|   â†ł `fixture_id` | number | Fixture the odd belongs to |
|   â†ł `external_id` | number | External id of the odd |
|   â†ł `market_id` | number | Market the odd belongs to |
|   â†ł `bookmaker_id` | number | Bookmaker offering the odd |
|   â†ł `label` | string | Outcome label \(e.g. 1, X, 2\) |
|   â†ł `value` | string | Decimal odds value |
|   â†ł `name` | string | Outcome name |
|   â†ł `sort_order` | number | Sort order of the odd |
|   â†ł `market_description` | string | Description of the market |
|   â†ł `probability` | string | Implied probability |
|   â†ł `dp3` | string | Decimal odds to 3 decimal places |
|   â†ł `fractional` | string | Fractional odds |
|   â†ł `american` | string | American/moneyline odds |
|   â†ł `winning` | boolean | Whether this is the winning outcome |
|   â†ł `suspended` | boolean | Whether the odd is suspended |
|   â†ł `stopped` | boolean | Whether the odd is stopped |
|   â†ł `total` | string | Total line for over/under markets |
|   â†ł `handicap` | string | Handicap line for handicap markets |
|   â†ł `participants` | string | Participant ids related to the outcome |

#### Input

| Parameter | Type | Required | Description |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Yes | Sportmonks API token |
| `fixtureId` | string | Yes | The unique id of the fixture |
| `include` | string | No | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response \(e.g. market;bookmaker\) |
| `filters` | string | No | Filters to apply \(e.g. markets:1,12 or bookmakers:2,14\) |

#### Output

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `premiumOdds` | array | Array of premium odd objects for the fixture |
|   â†ł `id` | number | Unique id of the odd |
|   â†ł `fixture_id` | number | Fixture the odd belongs to |
|   â†ł `market_id` | number | Market the odd belongs to |
|   â†ł `bookmaker_id` | number | Bookmaker offering the odd |
|   â†ł `label` | string | Outcome label |
|   â†ł `value` | string | Decimal odds value |
|   â†ł `name` | string | Outcome name |
|   â†ł `sort_order` | number | Sort order of the odd |
|   â†ł `market_description` | string | Description of the market |
|   â†ł `probability` | string | Implied probability \(e.g. 29.85%\) |
|   â†ł `dp3` | string | Decimal odds to 3 decimal places |
|   â†ł `fractional` | string | Fractional odds |
|   â†ł `american` | string | American/moneyline odds |
|   â†ł `stopped` | boolean | Whether the odd is stopped |
|   â†ł `total` | string | Total line for over/under markets |
|   â†ł `handicap` | string | Handicap line for handicap markets |
|   â†ł `created_at` | string | Timestamp the odd was created \(UTC\) |
|   â†ł `updated_at` | string | Timestamp the odd was last updated \(UTC\) |
|   â†ł `latest_bookmaker_update` | string | Bookmaker's own last-update timestamp \(UTC\) |

### `sportmonks_odds_get_updated_historical_odds_between`

Retrieve historical (premium) odds updated between two UNIX timestamps (max 5 minutes) from the Sportmonks Odds API

#### Input

| Parameter | Type | Required | Description |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Yes | Sportmonks API token |
| `fromTimestamp` | string | Yes | Start of the range as a UNIX timestamp \(e.g. 1767225600\) |
| `toTimestamp` | string | Yes | End of the range as a UNIX timestamp \(max 5 minutes after the start\) |
| `include` | string | No | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response \(e.g. odd\) |
| `filters` | string | No | Filters to apply \(e.g. winningOdds\) |
| `per_page` | string | No | Number of results per page \(max 50, default 25\) |
| `page` | string | No | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | No | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

#### Output

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `historicalOdds` | array | Array of historical premium odd value records updated within the time range |
|   â†ł `id` | number | Unique id of the history record |
|   â†ł `odd_id` | number | Premium odd this history record belongs to |
|   â†ł `value` | string | Historical decimal odds value |
|   â†ł `probability` | string | Implied probability at this point in time |
|   â†ł `dp3` | string | Decimal odds to 3 decimal places |
|   â†ł `fractional` | string | Fractional odds |
|   â†ł `american` | string | American/moneyline odds |
|   â†ł `bookmaker_update` | string | Bookmaker's update timestamp for this record \(UTC\) |

### `sportmonks_odds_get_updated_premium_odds_between`

Retrieve premium odds updated between two UNIX timestamps (max 5 minutes) from the Sportmonks Odds API

#### Input

| Parameter | Type | Required | Description |
| --------- | ---- | -------- | ----------- |
| `apiKey` | string | Yes | Sportmonks API token |
| `fromTimestamp` | string | Yes | Start of the range as a UNIX timestamp \(e.g. 1767225600\) |
| `toTimestamp` | string | Yes | End of the range as a UNIX timestamp \(max 5 minutes after the start\) |
| `include` | string | No | Semicolon-separated relations to enrich the response \(e.g. market;bookmaker\) |
| `filters` | string | No | Filters to apply \(e.g. markets:1,12 or bookmakers:2,14\) |
| `per_page` | string | No | Number of results per page \(max 50, default 25\) |
| `page` | string | No | Page number to retrieve |
| `order` | string | No | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

#### Output

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --------- | ---- | ----------- |
| `premiumOdds` | array | Array of premium odd objects updated within the time range |
|   â†ł `id` | number | Unique id of the odd |
|   â†ł `fixture_id` | number | Fixture the odd belongs to |
|   â†ł `market_id` | number | Market the odd belongs to |
|   â†ł `bookmaker_id` | number | Bookmaker offering the odd |
|   â†ł `label` | string | Outcome label |
|   â†ł `value` | string | Decimal odds value |
|   â†ł `name` | string | Outcome name |
|   â†ł `sort_order` | number | Sort order of the odd |
|   â†ł `market_description` | string | Description of the market |
|   â†ł `probability` | string | Implied probability \(e.g. 29.85%\) |
|   â†ł `dp3` | string | Decimal odds to 3 decimal places |
|   â†ł `fractional` | string | Fractional odds |
|   â†ł `american` | string | American/moneyline odds |
|   â†ł `stopped` | boolean | Whether the odd is stopped |
|   â†ł `total` | string | Total line for over/under markets |
|   â†ł `handicap` | string | Handicap line for handicap markets |
|   â†ł `created_at` | string | Timestamp the odd was created \(UTC\) |
|   â†ł `updated_at` | string | Timestamp the odd was last updated \(UTC\) |
|   â†ł `latest_bookmaker_update` | string | Bookmaker's own last-update timestamp \(UTC\) |

| `order` | string | No | Order direction \(asc or desc\) |

| Parameter | Type | Description |

|   â†ł `id` | number | Identifier of the usage record |
|   â†ł `endpoint` | string | Identifier of the requested endpoint |
|   â†ł `count` | number | Total calls for the given timeframe |
|   â†ł `entity` | string | The entity the rate limit applies on |
|   â†ł `remaining_requests` | number | Amount of requests remaining for the entity in the hourly rate limit |
|   â†ł `period_start` | number | Timestamp representing the aggregation start time |
|   â†ł `period_end` | number | Timestamp representing the aggregation end time |
